                   </a>

                    The latest COVID-19 economic package offers relief for single- and multiemployer pension funds.

                   <span class="feature-article-category">

                    </a>

                   <span class="text-gray divider-gray article-update-time" data-lastupdated="created--1616387380">

                  <h3 class="middle-article-headline">
                   <a class="font-bold" href="https://www.pionline.com/Eddy2021">
                    2021 Eddy Awards
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                  <div class="feature-article-summary pparagraph">
                   <p>
                    <i>
                     P&amp;I
                    </i>
                    spoke with plan sponsors and service providers to learn more about the strategies driving their award-winning communication campaigns.
                   </p>

                  <h3 class="middle-article-headline">
                   <a class="font-bold" href="https://www.pionline.com/investing/managers-keen-short-term-bonds-yields-climb">
                    Managers keen on short-term bonds as yields climb
                   </a>
                  </h3>
                  <div class="feature-article-summary pparagraph">
                   <p>
                    High-yield managers are set to focus on short-duration high-yield corporate bonds to avoid interest rate risk this year.
